There are basically no major faults with the facilities in the room. There are two TVs, which is convenient for two people to watch at the same time without grabbing each other. The toiletries are fixed in large bottles from Bai Ruide, smart toilets, and the bathtub is also very large. The only regret may be that I didn't use the Dyson hair dryer. The minibar is also free and the pineapple and lychee sodas in it are good.
There are only 78 rooms in the entire hotel. There are relatively few people and it covers a large area. It looks very empty. The hotel's service is very good and full of details, including greetings, pressing the elevator, and changing shoe covers when entering. Hygiene is also good, I can't fault it. The butler Maddie's service is also responsive. When we went to have dinner in the evening, the housekeeper Maddie contacted me specifically and said she wanted to give me welcome fruit, but my room showed Do Not Disturb and asked if I could come in. After returning from the meal, welcome fruits and chocolates were placed on the table, and we were turned down. We also had a Conrad bear on the bed. The service was really attentive.
As a resort hotel, the hotel's catering is very good, which is not easy, after all, the hotel's location is relatively remote. Dinner on the first day was at the hotel's Chinese restaurant. Although the dishes were not cheap, they tasted good, and specialties like veal were well-deserved. I especially want to praise the hotel's breakfast. Although there are very few varieties, it is very well made. The freshly made beef noodles alone are worthy of my praise. I showed them off for two nights, and the bread is also freshly baked. , very crispy.
Generally speaking, as a resort hotel, this hotel does well in terms of facilities, scenery, service, catering, etc. It is no wonder that it has been very popular since its opening more than 4 years ago. The only regret this time is that I didn‚Äôt bring my family dog ‚Äã‚Äãhere. I will definitely bring my dog ‚Äã‚Äãhere next time I have the opportunity.

All in all, my second trip to Conrad was a bit disappointing.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Suite
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Friends
info:6 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted July 18, 2023
msg:A true escape from the world. A destination to escape from.
Needless to say, the view of the hotel meanders up a short distance from the foot of the mountain
Only on the mountain road can we see the hotel complex, shaded by greenery, and the privacy is best protected. Two days, one night and three meals are served in the hotel. The coffee for breakfast is of better quality than the downtown hotel. The egg rolls are cooked just right. I ordered a bottle of wine for dinner and was rejected by the waiter.
I was informed that it was sold out, but I didn't expect the alternative recommended by the restaurant manager to taste better. The quality of ingredients can be found in such an isolated place, and the cost can be imagined.
Thank you for the memories the hotel brought us. I will come again when the weather is cold.
